// C:/Users/adm_a.zimmer/source/repos/water3d_monogame/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/base_lighttextures_base_light_runway_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/base_light/runway
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_runway_glow;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_runway;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_lightmap;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;
// stage3's externs
uniform texture stage3_runwayb;
uniform float3x2 stage3_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_runway_glow>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_runway>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage3_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage3_runwayb>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};
struct stage3_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD3;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
	stage3_input stage3;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 1;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 4;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 0.5 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage3.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_runway_glow
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_runway
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	// stage2_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv) * destination;

	// stage3_runwayb
	destination = (tex2D(stage3_sampler, input.stage3.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/adm_a.zimmer/source/repos/water3d_monogame/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/base_lighttextures_base_light_geolight_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/base_light/geolight
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_lightmap;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_geolight;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_geolight_glow;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_geolight>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_geolight_glow>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_geolight
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination) + (destination * tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv).a);

	// stage2_geolight_glow
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/adm_a.zimmer/source/repos/water3d_monogame/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/base_lighttextures_base_light_shi_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/base_light/shi
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_shi;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_shi;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_shi>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_shi>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 2;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 2;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 2;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 2;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_shi
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage1_shi
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	output.stage2.uv.y += 0 * gameTime;

	// stage3_
	destination = (tex2D(stage3_sampler, input.stage3.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;

// C:/Users/adm_a.zimmer/source/repos/water3d_monogame/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/base_lighttextures_base_light_ceil1_26_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/base_light/ceil1_26
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_ceil1_26;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_lightmap;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_ceil1_26>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.lightmapcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_ceil1_26
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}
